<Rating>1< /Rating>< review>
This was my go to nail place, and I know 20+ girls who go here and all love it. Eric, Ken, Kevin üëåüëå great at their art.  But I finally had a bad experience, and I'm afraid ill never go back. My nails started separating from their nail beds. I never had this happen before in the 6 full months that I started getting acrylics there. I went in for a fill, and when my polish came off I could see the damage, and you could tell he panicked as well. He started to file the inside of my nail, like under, and put super glue under my nails. Instead of helping me by suggesting I take them off and let them heal. He covered it up. I later googled it, and was horrified to find out this is common when using illegal product to make the acrylic. Someone people have a reaction, some don't. Or long periods of use can cause it as well when it comes to this illegal cheap product. I wish they didn't take advantage of their loyal paying customers. But it is what it is. Choose your nail place wisely ladies.< /review>

<Review>It is a beautiful setting but unfortunately there were certain things that were not represented correctly to us.  First, we were told that the venue had a relationship with three nearby hotels that would provide shuttle service for our guests.  The shuttles were only available to transport less than half our guests that had rooms.  Lomas Santa Fe was no help in this issue.  We spent an additional $325 on transportation.  Secondly, The food that we taste tested was not made by the same chef on the day of the wedding as he had quit.  We were not informed of this change.  The food was cold and bland.  Thirdly, ten days after our event the wedding coordinator contacted our daughter, the bride, to present an additional bill for drinks supposedly provided during the day as the wedding party got ready.  It would have been better to know of this at the time of service so we could understand what we are paying for.  At this time I have no idea if we received the drinks or not.

Lastly, I suppose that I am old fashion, but I do not like to be forced into paying a gratuity without regard for the quality of service.  It should be earned not expected.  It seems every venue does this, 21% gratuity which is also taxed, just beware to read the small print.< /Review>< GmapID>

I only rate 3 stars because they say food is served until 9:00 pm. I haven't been here in a little while and so I brought a friend with me so we can shoot some pool. My friend was hungry and we arrived inside at 8:50 pm and we asked what time do they stop serving food. We were told 9:00 pm. There was a lady in the kitchen and the bartender asked her if she could make anything and she told him the kitchen was closed. My friend said they just wanted something fried. She so the kitchen was closed. I've worked in a restaurant for 8 1/2 yrs and I know it's not hard to make some french fries and doesn't take long at all. Other than that it was a great evening and we had fun playing pool. They have 7 pool tables so we found one to play on easily. The bartender was friendly and the patrons were friendly and it wasn't very crowded which. I'm sure it may have gotten busier after we left. I'll definitely go back to play pool but probably not eat there since the kitchen closes before the posted time.</text>

INCREDIBLE EXPERIENCE!!!!

First things first ‚Äî the inside is literally like an international airport terminal. The design/architecture are awesome!!

Now onto Covid Safety. All the chairs were at least 6 feet apart from one another, and everybody in lines were 6 feet apart (there were little tape markers on the ground, each 6 feet away from the next). < review>
I arrived at 6:30am on a Friday to wait in line there was about 7 people already waiting. The security officer opened the gate and had us form 4 lines outside of the buildings entrance. The lines were divided by those that have an appointment, those that are using the kiosk, and for those that don‚Äôt have an appointment there was a line for registration and a line for CDL/CL. THEY ARE TAKING WALK INS. You cannot cut in-line the security officer was really on it making sure no one was cutting and everyone was in the line that they were supposed to be in. They started letting people in at 8am, starting with those that have an appointment(which wasn‚Äôt really much) and those using the kiosk and then 7 people from the line for registration and 7 people from the line for CL/CDL, about 5-10 minutes past then they do the same thing again, all from appt, then kiosk, then 7 reg, then 7 CL/CDL. I was in the line for registration, but I was also there for my CDL and I was able to do both. I did the registration and told the lady that I was also there for the CDL and she gave me a number I sat down and not even 5 minutes later called up to a window and then left like 5-10 minutes later. In all I waited an hour and 40 minutes to be seen, but 1 hour and 30 minutes from that 1 hour and 40 minutes is from arriving way before the actual opening time because I knew there was going to be a line. Inside the building I was able to get everything done in 10 minutes and leave without waiting no more that 5 minutes to be called up to a window. YOU CAN TAKE KIDS AND YOU HAVE TO WEAR A MASK INSIDE THE BUILDING. Over all it went really well, fast and everyone was really friendly and helpful. I say arrive early, I fell like the time that I arrived was a perfect time because when I left it was I believe 8:20am and there was two very long lines of people waiting outside the buildings entrance, wrapping outside the gates onto the sidewalk. I hope this was helpful.<//review>

Waited 4 hours here today and will have to start completely over again on Monday. It took over 1 hour just to get a number. The numbers are now your initials and the last four digits of your phone number, so you have no way to gauge if you are close to being called or not. At the 2 hour mark that can be problematic if you need the restroom, crave a smoke break or wanna run to the convenience store. I know I'm usually hesitant to leave the waiting area after waiting so long because I assume (and rightly so) that I could be called at any moment... Only to be kicking myself for not going to do it when they first had the urge after another hour passes.
Once my number was called (well after 5:00pm) I was relieved to find out I didn't have to take a test even though my license expired last August. I gave them everything they needed and was ready to pay. I slid my American Express Bluebird card and although I had plenty of money in my account, my transaction was denied. She told me they only take cash, check or debit. My bluebird card is an online "bank" account. They offer direct deposit, bill pay, paper checks, online check deposit/check"cashing", cash deposits via Walmart and other participating retailers, cash withdrawals from ATMs or cash back at stores... ITS A DEBIT CARD FROM A CHECKING ACCOUNT!...only there's no physical bank.

So...after ALL the waiting, I was told they could not save my info, give me an appointment, or help me in any way. I would have to start over completely on Monday. Everything I did today and all the waiting counts for NOTHING! They can't give me an appointment. They CAN'T (won't?) even do what they did for my boyfriend at the VERY BEGINNING OF THIS MONTH and let me pick up where I left off by going to the licensing window on Monday instead of waiting in the initial line that was all the way outside and down the entire length of the building.

Very dissatisfied and disappointed. I've been here 5 other times and NEVER had to wait more than an hour or two tops...4+hrs is pathetic! Hardly any workers until the very end of the day. If they had been working as fast and hard the whole day as they were at 5....it would have been a much faster experience.
to know they HAVE THE CAPACITY to be that efficient, BUT CHOOSE NOT TO is the reason I am so disgusted by the unnecessarily loooonnngggg wait and the overall visit today.</review>

<review>(Translated by Google) Very bad.
First, you need to fill out the application for a license renewal online, they are working with a minimum of staff, they offer you help but they are only about to fulfill their shift and collect their salary and nobody really helps you, they are not interested if you have or no computer or if you have a cell phone to fill out the application.
Second, you take them the documents after an hour of waiting to enter, you go in and they make you wait sitting for another hour when they attend to you and you give them all the documents they can't find you in the system and they ask if you got the application and if not the you filled up they send you to an area where there are computers and after queuing they tell you that the system is down.
Question? Whoever is sitting at the computer attending to him, the system does not crash and if I fill the application what is the function of the one who is sitting at the computer if I am doing the work of filling the application!
Is it just to verify that it is me with the documents?
Gentlemen, don't say you are here to help if you don't help.
Before the information was filled out on paper and we advanced with Eri technology with these people, you really don't see progress.
Conclusion, I do not recommend going to this place they will waste your time they are sitting with air conditioning and they do not care what you did to be able to be there, if you work if you asked permission if you have children or not.
